\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{abs\_tile()}{abs\_tile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::abs\+\_\+tile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs element-\/wise computation of absolute value on each element of a tile in DST register at index tile\+\_\+index. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Return value\+: None

Please refer to documentation for any\+\_\+init. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_ab3e5c0b33fb9768ebd6a7649dca13d56}\label{namespaceckernel_ab3e5c0b33fb9768ebd6a7649dca13d56}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!acquire\_dst@{acquire\_dst}}
\index{acquire\_dst@{acquire\_dst}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{acquire\_dst()}{acquire\_dst()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::acquire\+\_\+dst (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000001}{Deprecated}}]This function is deprecated, please use {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceckernel_a34467f46da4221ff3a2820ff1baec122}{tile\+\_\+regs\+\_\+acquire()}}} instead. See \href{https://github.com/tenstorrent/tt-metal/issues/5868\#issuecomment-2101726935}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/tenstorrent/tt-\/metal/issues/5868\#issuecomment-\/2101726935}}\end{DoxyRefDesc}


Acquires an exclusive lock on the internal DST register for the current Tensix core.

This register is an array of 16 tiles of 32x32 elements each. This is a blocking function, i.\+e. this function will wait until the lock is acquired.

This is only available on the compute engine.

Return value\+: None

How the destination register will be shared and synchronized between TRISC threads will depend on the compute kernel configuration. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_ae985587f12cada5d6a8af4c1a2252e92}\label{namespaceckernel_ae985587f12cada5d6a8af4c1a2252e92}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{add\_tiles()}{add\_tiles()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::add\+\_\+tiles (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb0,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb1,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{itile0,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{itile1,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ in0\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The identifier of the circular buffer (CB) containing A $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ in1\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The identifier of the circular buffer (CB) containing B $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ in0\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of tile A within the first CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ in1\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of tile B within the second CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ dst\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of the tile in DST REG for the result C $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the acquired size of DST REG $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_ab69ce76cfa211ae46dea6f04035a8050}\label{namespaceckernel_ab69ce76cfa211ae46dea6f04035a8050}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!add\_tiles\_bcast@{add\_tiles\_bcast}}
\index{add\_tiles\_bcast@{add\_tiles\_bcast}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{add\_tiles\_bcast()}{add\_tiles\_bcast()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$Broadcast\+Type t\+Bcast\+Dim$>$ \\
void ckernel\+::add\+\_\+tiles\+\_\+bcast (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb0,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb1,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{itile0,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{itile1,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This documentation applies to either one of the 3 broadcast operation variants -\/ {\itshape add\+\_\+tiles\+\_\+bcast}, {\itshape sub\+\_\+tiles\+\_\+bcast} and {\itshape mul\+\_\+tiles\+\_\+bcast}.

The description below describes {\itshape add\+\_\+tiles\+\_\+bcast}, the other 2 operations use the same definition with the corresponding substitution of the math operator.

Performs a broadcast-\/operation {\itshape C=A+B} of tiles in two CBs at given indices and writes the result to the DST register at index dst\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Broadcasting semantics are defined as follows\+:

For {\itshape dim==Broadcast\+Type\+::\+COL}, the input in {\itshape B} is expected to be a single tile with a filled 0-\/column and zeros elsewhere. The result is {\itshape C\mbox{[}h, w\mbox{]} = A\mbox{[}h,w\mbox{]} + B\mbox{[}w\mbox{]}}

For {\itshape dim==Dim\+::C}, the input in {\itshape B} is expected to be a single tile with a filled 0-\/row, and zeros elsewhere. The result is {\itshape C\mbox{[}h, w\mbox{]} = A\mbox{[}h,w\mbox{]} + B\mbox{[}h\mbox{]}}

For {\itshape dim==Dim\+::\+RC}, the input in {\itshape B} is expected to be a single tile with a filled single value at location \mbox{[}0,0\mbox{]}, and zeros elsewhere. The result is {\itshape C\mbox{[}h, w\mbox{]} = A\mbox{[}h,w\mbox{]} + B\mbox{[}0,0\mbox{]}}

Return value\+: None

DOX-\/\+TODO(AP)\+: verify that the bcast tile is actually required to be filled with zeros.

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ t\+Bcast\+Dim $\vert$ Broadcast dimension $\vert$ Broadcast\+Type $\vert$ One of Dim\+::R, Dim\+::C, Dim\+::\+RC. $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ in0\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The identifier of the circular buffer (CB) containing A $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ in1\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The indentifier of the circular buffer (CB) containing B $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ in0\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of tile A within the first CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ in1\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of tile B within the second CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ dst\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of the tile in DST REG for the result C $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the acquired size of DST REG $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_ac6a07f0334b79f3a1945e988bed27e95}\label{namespaceckernel_ac6a07f0334b79f3a1945e988bed27e95}}

Please refer to documentation for any\+\_\+init. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a9f5d8b2767ab4f1e188aac1ee4a8c744}\label{namespaceckernel_a9f5d8b2767ab4f1e188aac1ee4a8c744}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!binary\_dest\_reuse\_tiles@{binary\_dest\_reuse\_tiles}}
\index{binary\_dest\_reuse\_tiles@{binary\_dest\_reuse\_tiles}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{binary\_dest\_reuse\_tiles()}{binary\_dest\_reuse\_tiles()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$Eltwise\+Binary\+Type eltwise\+\_\+binary\+\_\+type = ELWADD, Eltwise\+Binary\+Reuse\+Dest\+Type binary\+\_\+reuse\+\_\+dest = Eltwise\+Binary\+Reuse\+Dest\+Type\+::\+NONE$>$ \\
void ckernel\+::binary\+\_\+dest\+\_\+reuse\+\_\+tiles (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{in\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{in\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{dst\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs element-\/wise binary operations, such as multiply, add, or sub of tiles. If binary\+\_\+reuse\+\_\+dest = Eltwise\+Binary\+Reuse\+Dest\+Type\+::\+DST\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+SRCA, then the tile specified by idst will be loaded from the DST register buffer into SRCA. The binary operation will operate on SRCA \& SRCB inputs, and the result will be written back to the DST register buffer specified by idst. Similar to DST\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+SRCA, if binary\+\_\+reuse\+\_\+dest = Eltwise\+Binary\+Reuse\+Dest\+Type\+::\+DST\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+SRCB, then tile specified by idst will be loaded from the DST into SRCB register buffer. DST\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+SRCB feature is not available for Grayskull, only Wormhole.

Eltwise\+Binary\+Reuse\+Dest\+Type\+::\+DST\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+SRCA and Eltwise\+Binary\+Reuse\+Dest\+Type\+::\+DST\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+SRCB assume that another operation has populated the dest register, otherwise dest will contain zeroes.

The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ in\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The identifier of the circular buffer (CB) containing A $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ in\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of tile A within the first CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ dst\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of tile B that will be moved to Src reg, and the index of the tile in DST REG for the result C $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the acquired size of DST REG $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a1ca6439309935d12d0f15ca795bb8985}\label{namespaceckernel_a1ca6439309935d12d0f15ca795bb8985}}

Init function for all binary ops Followed by the specific init required with an opcode (binrary\+\_\+op\+\_\+specific\+\_\+init) $\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ icb0 $\vert$ The identifier of the circular buffer (CB) containing A $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ icb1 $\vert$ The identifier of the circular buffer (CB) containing B $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ ocb $\vert$ The identifier of the circular buffer (CB) containing output $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31, defaults to CB 16 $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_ae239860fe24a16896deca931882e7bd6}\label{namespaceckernel_ae239860fe24a16896deca931882e7bd6}}

\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!cb\_get\_tile@{cb\_get\_tile}}
\index{cb\_get\_tile@{cb\_get\_tile}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cb\_get\_tile()}{cb\_get\_tile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::cb\+\_\+get\+\_\+tile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{cb\+\_\+id,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{index,  }\item[{volatile void $\ast$}]{p\+\_\+tile }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sends the pointer to the given tile index of the specified CB from the UNPACK thread to the MATH and PACK threads, using mailbox writes. Also posts UNPACK\+\_\+\+OPERAND\+\_\+\+SYNC semaphore for each of these threads.

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The index of the cirular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ index $\vert$ The tile index within the CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ It must be less or equal than the size of the CB (the total number of tiles that fit into the CB) $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ p\+\_\+tile $\vert$ The pointer that will be populated $\vert$ void$\ast$ $\vert$ N/A $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a09e8d82ba4b886f8e90eec038735d759}\label{namespaceckernel_a09e8d82ba4b886f8e90eec038735d759}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!cb\_pop\_front@{cb\_pop\_front}}
\index{cb\_pop\_front@{cb\_pop\_front}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cb\_pop\_front()}{cb\_pop\_front()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::cb\+\_\+pop\+\_\+front (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{cbid,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ntiles }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Pops a specified number of tiles from the front of the specified CB. This also frees this number of tiles in the circular buffer. This call is used by the consumer to free up the space in the CB.

We use the convention that the producer pushes tiles into the “back” of the CB queue and the consumer consumes tiles from the “front” of the CB queue.

Note that the act of reading of the tile data from the CB does not free up the space in the CB. Waiting on available tiles and popping them is separated in order to allow the consumer to\+: 1) read the tile data from the CB via multiple reads of sub-\/tiles 2) access the tiles (or their sub-\/tiles) that are visible to the consumer by random access of the valid section of the CB

Important note\+: This operation updates the read pointer of the CB, the CB pointer can only be updated from one thread at a time. Example\+: if compute kernel has cb\+\_\+pop\+\_\+front(input\+\_\+id, 1) and writer kernel also has cb\+\_\+pop\+\_\+front(input\+\_\+id, 1), these calls will produce non-\/deterministic behavior because cb pointers are not synchronized across threads. Per circular buffer index, only have one thread pop tiles to update the read pointer

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The index of the cirular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ ntiles $\vert$ The number of tiles to be popped $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ It must be less or equal than the size of the CB (the total number of tiles that fit into the CB) $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_af6f81e4da52b94a5397f904d446808c9}\label{namespaceckernel_af6f81e4da52b94a5397f904d446808c9}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!cb\_push\_back@{cb\_push\_back}}
\index{cb\_push\_back@{cb\_push\_back}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cb\_push\_back()}{cb\_push\_back()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::cb\+\_\+push\+\_\+back (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{cbid,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ntiles }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Pushes a given number of tiles in the back of the specified CB’s queue. Decreases the available space in the circular buffer by this number of tiles. This call is used by the producer to make the tiles visible to the consumer of the CB.

We use the convention that the producer pushes tiles into the “back” of the CB queue and the consumer consumes tiles from the “front” of the CB queue.

Note that the act of writing the tile data into the CB does not make the tiles visible to the consumer. Writing of the tiles and pushing is separated to allow the producer to\+: 1) write the tile data to the CB via multiple writes of sub-\/tiles 2) modify tiles (or sub-\/tiles) by random access of the valid section of the CB

Important note\+: This operation updates the write pointer of the CB, the CB pointer can only be updated from one thread at a time. Example\+: if compute kernel has cb\+\_\+push\+\_\+back(output\+\_\+id, 1) and reader kernel also has cb\+\_\+push\+\_\+back(output\+\_\+id, 1), these calls will produce non-\/deterministic behavior because cb pointers are not synchronized across threads. Per circular buffer index, only have one thread push tiles to update the write pointer

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The index of the cirular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ ntiles $\vert$ The number of tiles to be pushed $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ It must be less or equal than the size of the CB (the total number of tiles that fit into the CB) $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_ab833f2a940d6668f992dd77ca06ed03d}\label{namespaceckernel_ab833f2a940d6668f992dd77ca06ed03d}}

\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!cb\_reserve\_back@{cb\_reserve\_back}}
\index{cb\_reserve\_back@{cb\_reserve\_back}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cb\_reserve\_back()}{cb\_reserve\_back()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::cb\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+back (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{cbid,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ntiles }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

A blocking call that waits for the specified number of tiles to be free in the specified circular buffer. This call is used by the producer to wait for the consumer to consume (ie. free up) the specified number of tiles.

CB total size must be an even multiple of the argument passed to this call.

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The index of the cirular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ ntiles $\vert$ The number of free tiles to wait for $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ It must be less or equal than the size of the CB (the total number of tiles that fit into the CB) $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a2d20635facce5ae4c7ee121028740b38}\label{namespaceckernel_a2d20635facce5ae4c7ee121028740b38}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!cb\_wait\_front@{cb\_wait\_front}}
\index{cb\_wait\_front@{cb\_wait\_front}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cb\_wait\_front()}{cb\_wait\_front()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::cb\+\_\+wait\+\_\+front (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{cbid,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ntiles }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

A blocking call that waits for the specified number of tiles to be available in the specified circular buffer (CB). This call is used by the consumer of the CB to wait for the producer to fill the CB with at least the specfied number of tiles. Important note\+: in case multiple calls of cb\+\_\+wait\+\_\+front(n) are issued without a paired \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceckernel_a09e8d82ba4b886f8e90eec038735d759}{cb\+\_\+pop\+\_\+front()}} call, n is expected to be incremented by the user to be equal to a cumulative total of tiles. Example\+: 4 calls of cb\+\_\+wait\+\_\+front(8) followed by a cb\+\_\+pop\+\_\+front(32) would produce incorrect behavior. Instead 4 calls of \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceckernel_a2d20635facce5ae4c7ee121028740b38}{cb\+\_\+wait\+\_\+front()}} waiting on 8, 16, 24, 32 tiles should be issued.

Important note\+: number of tiles used in all cb\+\_\+$\ast$ calls must evenly divide the cb size and must be the same number in all cb\+\_\+wait\+\_\+front calls in the same kernel. Example 1\+: cb\+\_\+wait\+\_\+front(32), cb\+\_\+wait\+\_\+front(40), cb\+\_\+pop\+\_\+front(32+8) tiles on a CB of size 64 would produce incorrect behavior. Example 2\+: cb\+\_\+wait\+\_\+front(3) on a cb of size 32 would also produce incorrect behavior. These limitations are due to performance optimizations in the CB implementation.

Important note\+: CB total size must be an even multiple of the argument passed to this call.

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The index of the cirular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ ntiles $\vert$ The number of tiles to wait for $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ It must be less or equal than the size of the CB (the total number of tiles that fit into the CB) $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a8babb406a90ed09abdce7a53d3e20b84}\label{namespaceckernel_a8babb406a90ed09abdce7a53d3e20b84}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{copy\_block\_matmul\_partials()}{copy\_block\_matmul\_partials()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::copy\+\_\+block\+\_\+matmul\+\_\+partials (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{in\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{start\+\_\+in\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{start\+\_\+dst\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ntiles }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a150166792eaa318a5837165e71e8b44c}\label{namespaceckernel_a150166792eaa318a5837165e71e8b44c}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!copy\_tile@{copy\_tile}}
\index{copy\_tile@{copy\_tile}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{copy\_tile()}{copy\_tile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::copy\+\_\+tile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{in\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{in\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{dst\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies a single tile from the specified input CB and writes the result to DST at a specified index. The function will employ unpacker to first unpack into SRC registers and then perform move into DST registers, at a specified index. For the in\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index to be valid for this call, cb\+\_\+wait\+\_\+front(n) had to be previously called to ensure that at least some number n\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}0 of tiles are available in the input CB. The CB index 0 then references the first tile in the received section of the CB, up to index n-\/1 (in a FIFO order). The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via acquire\+\_\+dst call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Data type $\vert$ Valid range $\vert$ required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ in\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The identifier of the source circular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ Yes $\vert$ $\vert$ in\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of the tile to copy from the input CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ Yes $\vert$ $\vert$ dst\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of the tile in the DST register $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the DST register (16) $\vert$ Yes $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_aea570483ca5371db26adbdb562bdc640}\label{namespaceckernel_aea570483ca5371db26adbdb562bdc640}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::cos\+\_\+tile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs element-\/wise computation of the trigonometric cosine operation on each element of a tile in DST register at index tile\+\_\+index. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Performs element-\/wise computation of elu (relu(x) + slope$\ast$(exp(x) -\/ 1)$\ast$(x \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= 0 )) on each element of a tile in DST register at index tile\+\_\+index. $\vert$ Must be less than the acquired size of DST REG $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ transpose $\vert$ The transpose flag for performing transpose operation on tiles in B. $\vert$ bool $\vert$ Must be true or false $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ ct\+\_\+dim $\vert$ The coloumn dimension for the output block. $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be equal to block B column dimension $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ rt\+\_\+dim $\vert$ The row dimension for the output block. $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be equal to block A row dimension $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ kt\+\_\+dim $\vert$ The inner dimension. $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be equal to block A column dimension $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_aac63a0fae82e1b790a1f6b3a3d8d600f}\label{namespaceckernel_aac63a0fae82e1b790a1f6b3a3d8d600f}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!matmul\_pack\_tile@{matmul\_pack\_tile}}
\index{matmul\_pack\_tile@{matmul\_pack\_tile}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{matmul\_pack\_tile()}{matmul\_pack\_tile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::matmul\+\_\+pack\+\_\+tile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ifrom\+\_\+dst,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ntiles }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies a block of tiles from the DST register buffer at a start index to a specified CB at a given start index. cb\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+back(n) had to be called first to reserve at least some number n\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}0 of tiles in the output CB. The out\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index = 0 then references the first tile in the reserved section of the CB, up to index n-\/1 that will then be visible to the consumer in the same order after a cb\+\_\+push\+\_\+back call. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Each subsequent pack call will increment the write pointer in the cb by ntiles size. The pointer is then again set to a valid position with space for n reserved tiles by another cb\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+back call.

Operates in tandem with functions cb\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+back and cb\+\_\+push\+\_\+back.

A typical use case is first the producer ensures that there is a number of tiles available in the buffer via cb\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+back, then the producer uses the matmul\+\_\+pack\+\_\+tile call to copy a block of tiles from the DST slots to the slots in reserved space and finally cb\+\_\+push\+\_\+back is called to announce visibility of the reserved section of the circular buffer to the consumer.

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ ifrom\+\_\+dst $\vert$ The index of the tile in the DST register $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the DST register (16) $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ icb $\vert$ The identifier of the output circular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ ntiles $\vert$ The number of tiles to copy from DST to CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_ae3b5c274614aec08a77df1f78829c39d}\label{namespaceckernel_ae3b5c274614aec08a77df1f78829c39d}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!matmul\_tiles@{matmul\_tiles}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{matmul\_tiles()}{matmul\_tiles()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::matmul\+\_\+tiles (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{in0\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{in1\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{in0\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{in1\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{transpose }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs tile-\/sized matrix multiplication {\itshape C=A$\ast$B} between the tiles in two specified input CBs and writes the result to DST. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ in0\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The identifier of the first input circular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ in1\+\_\+cb\+\_\+id $\vert$ The identifier of the second input circular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ in0\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of the tile A from the first input CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ in1\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of the tile B from the second input CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ dst\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index $\vert$ The index of the tile in DST REG to which the result C will be written. $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the acquired size of DST REG $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a11c225636a89c5fbc8e3ab0f17902f88}\label{namespaceckernel_a11c225636a89c5fbc8e3ab0f17902f88}}

The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::pack\+\_\+reconfig\+\_\+l1\+\_\+acc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{l1\+\_\+acc\+\_\+en }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Helper function to reconfigure packer l1 accumulation flag \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a63c43acd48809eac8f0fd79a09cac7b7}\label{namespaceckernel_a63c43acd48809eac8f0fd79a09cac7b7}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!pack\_tile@{pack\_tile}}
\index{pack\_tile@{pack\_tile}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pack\_tile()}{pack\_tile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$bool out\+\_\+of\+\_\+order\+\_\+output = false$>$ \\
void ckernel\+::pack\+\_\+tile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ifrom\+\_\+dst,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb,  }\item[{std\+::uint32\+\_\+t}]{output\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies a single tile from the DST register buffer at a specified index to a specified CB at a given index. For the out\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index to be valid for this call, cb\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+back(n) has to be called first to reserve at least some number n \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0 of tiles in the output CB. out\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index = 0 then references the first tile in the reserved section of the CB, up to index n -\/ 1, which will then be visible to the consumer in the same order after a cb\+\_\+push\+\_\+back call. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Each subsequent pack call will increment the write pointer in the cb by single tile size. The pointer is then again set to a valid position with space for n reserved tiles by another cb\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+back call.

Operates in tandem with functions cb\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+back and cb\+\_\+push\+\_\+back.

A typical use case is first the producer ensures that there is a number of tiles available in the buffer via cb\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+back, then the producer uses the pack\+\_\+tile call to copy a tile from one of DST slots to a slot in reserved space and finally cb\+\_\+push\+\_\+back is called to announce visibility of the reserved section of the circular buffer to the consumer.

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ ifrom\+\_\+dst $\vert$ The index of the tile in the DST register $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the DST register (16) $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ icb $\vert$ The identifier of the output circular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ icb\+\_\+tile $\vert$ The index of the tile in the output CB to copy to $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a61fe18515827e58bdfea82fa99daee38}\label{namespaceckernel_a61fe18515827e58bdfea82fa99daee38}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!power\_tile@{power\_tile}}
\index{power\_tile@{power\_tile}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{power\_tile()}{power\_tile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::power\+\_\+tile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{param0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs element-\/wise computation of power operation (x $^\wedge$(const param0)) value on each element of a tile in DST register at index tile\+\_\+index. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Return value\+: None

\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!recip\_tile@{recip\_tile}}
\index{recip\_tile@{recip\_tile}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{recip\_tile()}{recip\_tile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::recip\+\_\+tile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs element-\/wise computation of the reciprocal on each element of a tile in DST register at index tile\+\_\+index. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine. Only works for Float32, Float16\+\_\+b, Bfp8\+\_\+b data formats for full accuracy.

Return value\+: None

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a38f4526f08151193fd4a2b8006c3543e}\label{namespaceckernel_a38f4526f08151193fd4a2b8006c3543e}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!reduce\_tile@{reduce\_tile}}
\index{reduce\_tile@{reduce\_tile}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{reduce\_tile()}{reduce\_tile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$Pool\+Type reduce\+\_\+type = REDUCE\+\_\+\+OP, Reduce\+Dim reduce\+\_\+dim = REDUCE\+\_\+\+DIM$>$ \\
void ckernel\+::reduce\+\_\+tile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb0,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb1,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{itile0,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{itile1,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs a reduction operation {\itshape B = reduce(\+A)} using reduce\+\_\+func for dimension reduction on a tile in the CB at a given index and writes the result to the DST register at index {\itshape dst\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index}. Reduction can be either of type {\itshape Reduce\+::R}, {\itshape Reduce\+::C} or {\itshape Reduce\+::\+RC}, identifying the dimension(s) to be reduced in size to 1. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call.

The templates takes reduce\+\_\+type which can be Reduce\+Func\+::\+Sum, Reduce\+Func\+::\+Max and reduce\+\_\+dim which can be Reduce\+::R, Reduce\+::C, Reduce\+::\+RC. They can also be specified by defines REDUCE\+\_\+\+OP and REDUCE\+\_\+\+DIM.

This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ icb0 $\vert$ The identifier of the circular buffer (CB) containing A $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ icb1 $\vert$ CB for Scaling factor applied to each element of the result. $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ itile0 $\vert$ The index of the tile within the first CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ itile1 $\vert$ The index of the tile within the scaling factor CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ idst $\vert$ The index of the tile in DST REG for the result $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the acquired size of DST REG $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a12ea45120e9ffcb785c88effcbd9e42b}\label{namespaceckernel_a12ea45120e9ffcb785c88effcbd9e42b}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_aca8a1c47b441f374e4ad21ed8d2f8a4e}\label{namespaceckernel_aca8a1c47b441f374e4ad21ed8d2f8a4e}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!release\_dst@{release\_dst}}
\index{release\_dst@{release\_dst}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{release\_dst()}{release\_dst()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::release\+\_\+dst (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000002}{Deprecated}}]This function is deprecated, please use {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceckernel_addd3679665da343bd51f76ced7154c4a}{tile\+\_\+regs\+\_\+release()}}} instead. See \href{https://github.com/tenstorrent/tt-metal/issues/5868\#issuecomment-2101726935}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/tenstorrent/tt-\/metal/issues/5868\#issuecomment-\/2101726935}}\end{DoxyRefDesc}


Releases the exclusive lock on the internal DST register for the current Tensix core. This lock had to be previously acquired with acquire\+\_\+dst. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Return value\+: None

How the destination register will be shared and synchronized between TRISC threads will depend on the compute kernel configuration. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_ab022361921e28e620e0aa64449d707a8}\label{namespaceckernel_ab022361921e28e620e0aa64449d707a8}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!relu\_max\_tile@{relu\_max\_tile}}
\index{relu\_max\_tile@{relu\_max\_tile}!ckernel@{ckernel}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::relu\+\_\+max\+\_\+tile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{param0 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs element-\/wise computation of relu max (relu(max(x, upper\+\_\+limit))) on each element of a tile in DST register at index tile\+\_\+index. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Return value\+: None

\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!tilizeA\_B\_reduce\_init@{tilizeA\_B\_reduce\_init}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$bool neginf\+\_\+srcA = true, bool zero\+\_\+src\+A\+\_\+reduce = false$>$ \\
void ckernel\+::tilize\+A\+\_\+\+B\+\_\+reduce\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb0,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb1\+\_\+scaler,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{block,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ocb = {\ttfamily 16},  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{num\+\_\+faces = {\ttfamily 4},  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{face\+\_\+r\+\_\+dim = {\ttfamily 16} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Initialize the tilize operation. To be called once at beginning of a kernel. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_aa5210fb3aea6ef6c09eba614308a25c5}\label{namespaceckernel_aa5210fb3aea6ef6c09eba614308a25c5}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!topk\_local\_sort@{topk\_local\_sort}}
\index{topk\_local\_sort@{topk\_local\_sort}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{topk\_local\_sort()}{topk\_local\_sort()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::topk\+\_\+local\+\_\+sort (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst,  }\item[{int}]{idir,  }\item[{int}]{i\+\_\+end\+\_\+phase,  }\item[{int}]{i\+\_\+start\+\_\+phase = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{int}]{i\+\_\+end\+\_\+step = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{int}]{i\+\_\+start\+\_\+step = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs local sort stage of TopK algorithm on the two data tiles and two index tiles that are pre-\/loaded in DST register. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

The algorithm used to implement TopK is found here\+: \href{https://anilshanbhag.in/static/papers/gputopk_sigmod18.pdf}{\texttt{ https\+://anilshanbhag.\+in/static/papers/gputopk\+\_\+sigmod18.\+pdf}}

The local sort stage sorts the data into length-\/K subsequences of alternating directions, in place. If i\+\_\+start\+\_\+phase != i\+\_\+end\+\_\+phase, all phases in the range i\+\_\+start\+\_\+phase to i\+\_\+end\+\_\+phase (inclusive) are computed. If i\+\_\+start\+\_\+phase == i\+\_\+end\+\_\+phase, only that phase is computed, with i\+\_\+start\+\_\+step and i\+\_\+end\+\_\+step defining how many steps are computed. This can be used to extend the OP support for cases when K \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 64.

Note that the two data tiles need to be loaded into the DST register before the invocation of this call. The corresponding index tiles should also be loaded in with the data tiles, at a DST offset of 2 tiles.

Note that local sort is done across columns on 64 values spanning across 2 tiles.

Note\+: idist should be set to 0

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ idst $\vert$ The index of the tile in DST register buffer to perform the computation on $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the DST register buffer $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ idir $\vert$ The sorting direction of the local sort (0 == decreasing, 1 == increasing) $\vert$ int32 $\vert$ 0 to 1 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ i\+\_\+end\+\_\+phase $\vert$ The end phase of the local sort (should be set to log(\+K)-\/1) $\vert$ int32 $\vert$ 1 to 5 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ i\+\_\+start\+\_\+phase $\vert$ The start phase of the local sort (should be set to 0) $\vert$ int32 $\vert$ 0 to 5 $\vert$ False $\vert$ $\vert$ i\+\_\+end\+\_\+step $\vert$ The end step to perform if i\+\_\+start\+\_\+phase == i\+\_\+end\+\_\+phase $\vert$ int32 $\vert$ 4 to 6 $\vert$ False $\vert$ $\vert$ i\+\_\+start\+\_\+step $\vert$ The start step to perform if i\+\_\+start\+\_\+phase == i\+\_\+end\+\_\+phase $\vert$ int32 $\vert$ 4 to 6 $\vert$ False $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a2938cab3b09934d9f491eb7e8e46a9c6}\label{namespaceckernel_a2938cab3b09934d9f491eb7e8e46a9c6}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!topk\_merge@{topk\_merge}}
\index{topk\_merge@{topk\_merge}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{topk\_merge()}{topk\_merge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::topk\+\_\+merge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst,  }\item[{int}]{m\+\_\+iter,  }\item[{int}]{k }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs merge stage of TopK algorithm on the two data tiles and two index tiles that are pre-\/loaded in DST register. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

The merge stage combines length-\/K subsequences that are 2$^\wedge$m\+\_\+iter apart, such that the first subsequence receives the top K values, and the second subsequence receives the bottom K values.

Note that the two data tiles need to be loaded into the DST register before the invocation of this call. The corresponding index tiles should also be loaded in with the data tiles, at a DST offset of 2 tiles.

Note that merge is done across columns on values spanning across 2 tiles.

Note\+: idist should be set to 0

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ idst $\vert$ The index of the tile in DST register buffer to perform the computation on $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the DST register buffer $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ m\+\_\+iter $\vert$ The index of the merge \& rebuild iteration of the algorithm $\vert$ int32 $\vert$ 0 to 9 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ k $\vert$ The number of sorted values to return $\vert$ int32 $\vert$ \{4, 8, 16, 32, 64\} $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_ae1cbdb83cc5bc20da93967c2252354b8}\label{namespaceckernel_ae1cbdb83cc5bc20da93967c2252354b8}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!topk\_rebuild@{topk\_rebuild}}
\index{topk\_rebuild@{topk\_rebuild}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{topk\_rebuild()}{topk\_rebuild()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::topk\+\_\+rebuild (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst,  }\item[{bool}]{idir,  }\item[{int}]{m\+\_\+iter,  }\item[{int}]{k,  }\item[{int}]{logk,  }\item[{int}]{skip\+\_\+second }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs rebuild stage of TopK algorithm on the two data tiles and two index tiles that are pre-\/loaded in DST register. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

The rebuild stage sorts the length-\/K subsequences that are 2$^\wedge$(m\+\_\+iter+1) apart, such that they alternate directions.

Note that the two data tiles need to be loaded into the DST register before the invocation of this call. The corresponding index tiles should also be loaded in with the data tiles, at a DST offset of 2 tiles.

Note that rebuild is done across columns on values spanning across 2 tiles.

Note\+: idist should be set to 0

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Type $\vert$ Valid Range $\vert$ Required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ idst $\vert$ The index of the tile in DST register buffer to perform the computation on $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the DST register buffer $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ idir $\vert$ The sorting direction of the local sort (0 == decreasing, 1 == increasing) $\vert$ bool $\vert$ 0 to 1 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ m\+\_\+iter $\vert$ The index of the merge \& rebuild iteration of the algorithm $\vert$ int32 $\vert$ 0 to 9 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ k $\vert$ The number of sorted values to return $\vert$ int32 $\vert$ \{4, 8, 16, 32, 64\} $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ logk $\vert$ The log of K $\vert$ int32 $\vert$ 2 to 6 $\vert$ True $\vert$ $\vert$ skip\+\_\+second $\vert$ Whether or not to skip second tile $\vert$ int32 $\vert$ 0 to 1 $\vert$ True $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a53c812a947f6d756ea625b7361174037}\label{namespaceckernel_a53c812a947f6d756ea625b7361174037}}

Performs a first-\/call or switch-\/from-\/another-\/op tile hw reconfiguration step needed for transpose\+\_\+wh to be executed correctly. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_ab885f1c61cacad96feb21ff8c9b099aa}\label{namespaceckernel_ab885f1c61cacad96feb21ff8c9b099aa}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!transpose\_wh\_tile@{transpose\_wh\_tile}}
\index{transpose\_wh\_tile@{transpose\_wh\_tile}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{transpose\_wh\_tile()}{transpose\_wh\_tile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::transpose\+\_\+wh\+\_\+tile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{itile,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{idst }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs a 32x32 transpose operation {\itshape B\mbox{[}w,h\mbox{]} = A\mbox{[}h,w\mbox{]}} on a tile in the CB at a given index and writes the result to the DST register at index dst\+\_\+tile\+\_\+index. The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call.

This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::unpack\+\_\+tilize\+A\+\_\+\+B\+\_\+block (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb0,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb1,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{block,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{tile\+\_\+idx\+\_\+b,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{num\+\_\+faces = {\ttfamily 4},  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{srca\+\_\+face\+\_\+r\+\_\+dim = {\ttfamily 16} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_a100bc7f788be0c8206261722ac613de7}\label{namespaceckernel_a100bc7f788be0c8206261722ac613de7}} 
\index{ckernel@{ckernel}!unpack\_tilizeA\_B\_dot\_product\_block@{unpack\_tilizeA\_B\_dot\_product\_block}}
\index{unpack\_tilizeA\_B\_dot\_product\_block@{unpack\_tilizeA\_B\_dot\_product\_block}!ckernel@{ckernel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpack\_tilizeA\_B\_dot\_product\_block()}{unpack\_tilizeA\_B\_dot\_product\_block()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ckernel\+::unpack\+\_\+tilize\+A\+\_\+\+B\+\_\+dot\+\_\+product\+\_\+block (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb0,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{icb1,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{block,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{tile\+\_\+idx\+\_\+b,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{num\+\_\+faces = {\ttfamily 4} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Loads a single tile from the specified input CBs into SRCA and SRCB. The function will employ one unpacker to unpack and tilize data from the first input CB into SRCA, and the second unpacker to unpack from the second input CB into SRCB. For the tile\+\_\+idx\+\_\+b and block to be valid for this call, cb\+\_\+wait\+\_\+front(n) had to be previously called on each input CB to ensure that at least some number n\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}0 of tiles are available in the input CBs. The CB index 0 then references the first tile in the received section of the CB, up to index n-\/1 (in a FIFO order). The DST register buffer must be in acquired state via {\itshape acquire\+\_\+dst} call. This call is blocking and is only available on the compute engine.

Return value\+: None

$\vert$ Argument $\vert$ Description $\vert$ Data type $\vert$ Valid range $\vert$ required $\vert$ $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $\vert$ icb0 $\vert$ The identifier of the source A circular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ Yes $\vert$ $\vert$ icb1 $\vert$ The identifier of the source B circular buffer (CB) $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 0 to 31 $\vert$ Yes $\vert$ $\vert$ block $\vert$ Size of tile block to work on for source A $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0 $\vert$ Yes $\vert$ $\vert$ tile\+\_\+idx\+\_\+b $\vert$ The index of the tile to copy from the source B input CB $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ Must be less than the size of the CB $\vert$ Yes $\vert$ $\vert$ num\+\_\+faces $\vert$ The number of faces to in each tile being unpacked $\vert$ uint32\+\_\+t $\vert$ 1 to 4 $\vert$ Yes $\vert$ \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceckernel_abdf529b965f1e85626342a4027d36461}\label{namespaceckernel_abdf529b965f1e85626342a4027d36461}}
